Each Wednesday in March, well be recognizing the women whove demanded their place in music history. <br>This week, we honor Joan Jett. A founding member of the Runaways, considered by many to be the first true all-female rock band, Jett created a sound and style all her own by infusing hard rock with energetic, curled-lip punk. Over the course of her career, she has established herself as a rock n roll icon, inspiring countless women to boldly and confidently assert their own musical vision.
